<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="initial-value" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Initial Value</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To set the radio group&#x27;s initial value, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultValue</code> prop to the value of the radio item to be selected by
default.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For a controlled Radio Group, the state is managed using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> prop, and updates when the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> event
handler is called:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the radio group is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useRadioGroup</code> hook. This
way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="disabled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#disabled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Disabled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To make a radio group disabled, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disabled</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="aschild" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#aschild"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>asChild</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RadioGroup.Item</code> component renders as a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> element by default. This ensures proper form semantics and
accessibility, as radio groups are form controls that require labels to provide meaningful context for users.</p>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">asChild</code> prop, you must <strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">render a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">label</code> element</strong> as the direct child of <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RadioGroup.Item</code> to
maintain valid HTML structure and accessibility compliance.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// INCORRECT usage ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.Item</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> asChild</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">div</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemControl</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">div</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.Item</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// CORRECT usage ✅</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.Item</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> asChild</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">label</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemControl</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">label</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.Item</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="hidden-input" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#hidden-input"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Hidden Input</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput</code> component renders a hidden HTML input element that enables proper form submission and
integration with native form behaviors. This component is essential for the radio group to function correctly as it:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Provides the underlying input element that browsers use for form submission</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Enables integration with form libraries and validation systems</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em">Ensures the radio group works with native form reset functionality</li>
</ul>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// INCORRECT usage ❌</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.Item</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemText</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// CORRECT usage ✅</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.Item</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">RadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>

<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior.</p><span class="text">For more details, read our<!-- --> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="link" href="/react/docs/guides/composition">Composition</a> <!-- -->guide.</span></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">API</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Property</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">value</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">string</code><p class="text">The current value of the radio group</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">setValue</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to set the value of the radio group</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">clearValue</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">VoidFunction</code><p class="text">Function to clear the value of the radio group</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">focus</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">VoidFunction</code><p class="text">Function to focus the radio group</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">getItemState</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(props: ItemProps) =&gt; ItemState</code><p class="text">Returns the state details of a radio input</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/radio/" class="link">Radio WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to either the checked radio item or the first radio item in the group.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Space</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">When focus is on an unchecked radio item, checks it.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm px_1">ArrowDown</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus and checks the next radio item in the group.</td></tr><tr radio item in the group.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div `defaultValue` prop to the value of the radio item to be selected by\ndefault.\n\n**Example: initial-value**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/radio-group'\nimport the `value` prop, and updates when the `onValueChange` event\nhandler is called:\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/radio-group'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n  const [value, setValue] = useState\u003cstring | null\u003e(null)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Root className={styles.Root} value={value} onValueChange={(e) =\u003e setValue(e.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n      {frameworks.map((framework) =\u003e (\n        \u003cRadioGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={framework} value={framework}\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl className={styles.ItemControl} /\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/radio-group'\nimport { For, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from This\nway you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup, useRadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/radio-group'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n  const radioGroup = useRadioGroup({ defaultValue: 'React' })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={radioGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cRadioGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n        {frameworks.map((framework) =\u003e (\n          \u003cRadioGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={framework} value={framework}\u003e\n            \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl className={styles.ItemControl} /\u003e\n            \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{framework}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n            \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n          \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n        ))}\n      \u003c/RadioGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e radioGroup.setValue('Solid')}\u003e\n        Set to Solid\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup, useRadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/radio-group'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport button \u003cRadioGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n        \u003cFor each={frameworks}\u003e\n          {(framework) =\u003e (\n            \u003cRadioGroup.Item \u003c/button\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RadioGroup, useRadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/radio-group'\nimport button })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"radioGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Label }}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n\n    \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"radioGroup.setValue('Solid')\"\u003eSet to Solid\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RadioGroup, useRadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/radio-group'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\n  const frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const radioGroup = useRadioGroup({ id, defaultValue: 'React' })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={radioGroup}\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n    {#each frameworks as framework}\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Item class={styles.Item} value={framework}\u003e\n        \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl class={styles.ItemControl} /\u003e\n        \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{framework}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n        \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n    {/each}\n  \u003c/RadioGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n\n  \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e radioGroup().setValue('Solid')}\u003eSet to Solid\u003c/button\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Disabled\n\nTo make a radio group disabled, set the `disabled` prop to `true`.\n\n**Example: disabled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/radio-group'\nimport styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Disabled = () =\u003e {\n  const frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n\n  return (\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"React\" disabled\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n      {frameworks.map((framework) =\u003e (\n        \u003cRadioGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={framework} value={framework}\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl className={styles.ItemControl} /\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText className={styles.ItemText}\u003e{framework}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n          \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/radio-group'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Disabled = () =\u003e {\n  const frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n\n  return (\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"React\" disabled\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cFor each={frameworks}\u003e\n        {(framework) =\u003e (\n          \u003cRadioGroup.Item class={styles.Item} value={framework}\u003e\n            \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl class={styles.ItemControl} /\u003e\n            \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{framework}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n            \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n          \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/For\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/radio-group'\nimport styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\nconst frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" default-value=\"React\" disabled\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Item v-for=\"framework in frameworks\" :key=\"framework\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :value=\"framework\"\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl :class=\"styles.ItemControl\" /\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText :class=\"styles.ItemText\"\u003e{{ framework }}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n  \u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RadioGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/radio-group'\n  import styles from 'styles/radio-group.module.css'\n\n  const frameworks = ['React', 'Solid', 'Vue']\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cRadioGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue=\"React\" disabled\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eFramework\u003c/RadioGroup.Label\u003e\n  {#each frameworks as framework}\n    \u003cRadioGroup.Item class={styles.Item} value={framework}\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl class={styles.ItemControl} /\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText class={styles.ItemText}\u003e{framework}\u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n  {/each}\n\u003c/RadioGroup.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n## Guides\n\n### asChild\n\nThe `RadioGroup.Item` component renders as a `label` element by default. This ensures proper form semantics and\naccessibility, as radio groups are form controls that require labels to provide meaningful context for users.\n\nWhen using the `asChild` prop, you must **render a `label` element** as the direct child of `RadioGroup.Item` to\nmaintain valid HTML structure and accessibility compliance.\n\n```tsx\n// INCORRECT usage ❌\n\u003cRadioGroup.Item asChild\u003e\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl /\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n\n// CORRECT usage ✅\n\u003cRadioGroup.Item asChild\u003e\n  \u003clabel\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n      \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl /\u003e\n    \u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n  \u003c/label\u003e\n\u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n```\n\n### Hidden Input\n\nThe `RadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput` component renders a hidden HTML input element that enables proper form submission and\nintegration with native form behaviors. This component is essential for the radio group to function correctly as it:\n\n- Provides the underlying input element that browsers use for form submission\n- Enables integration with form libraries and validation systems\n- Ensures the radio group works with native form reset functionality\n\n```tsx\n// INCORRECT usage ❌\n\u003cRadioGroup.Item\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl /\u003e\n  \u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n\u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n\n// CORRECT usage ✅\n\u003cRadioGroup.Item\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.ItemHiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003cRadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n    \u003cRadioGroup.ItemControl /\u003e\n  \u003c/RadioGroup.ItemText\u003e\n\u003c/RadioGroup.Item\u003e\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Props\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**Root Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `defaultValue` | `string` | No | The initial value of the checked radio when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the value of the radio group. |\n| `disabled` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the radio group will be disabled |\n| `form` | `string` | No | The associate form of the underlying input. |\n| `id` | `string` | No | The unique identifier of the machine. |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{\n  root: string\n  label: string\n  indicator: string\n  item: (value: string) =\u003e string\n  itemLabel: (value: string) =\u003e string\n  itemControl: (value: string) =\u003e string\n  itemHiddenInput: (value: string) =\u003e string\n}\u003e` | No | The ids of the elements in the radio. Useful for composition. |\n| `invalid` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the radio group is marked as invalid. |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name of the input fields in the radio\n(Useful for form submission). |\n| `onValueChange` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function called once a radio is checked |\n| `orientation` | `'horizontal' | 'vertical'` | No | Orientation of the radio group |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the radio group is read-only |\n| `required` | `boolean` | No | If `true`, the radio group is marked as required. |\n| `value` | `string` | No | The controlled value of the radio group |\n\n\n**Root Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | radio-group |\n| `[data-part]` | root |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the radio-group |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-invalid]` | Present when invalid |\n| `[data-required]` | Present when required |\n\n\n**Indicator Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n\n\n**Indicator Data Attributes:**\n\n| Attribute | Value |\n|-----------|-------|\n| `[data-scope]` | radio-group |\n| `[data-part]` | indicator |\n| `[data-disabled]` | Present when disabled |\n| `[data-orientation]` | The orientation of the indicator |\n\n\n**Indicator CSS Variables:**\n\n| Variable | Description |\n|----------|-------------|\n| `--transition-property` | The transition property value for the Indicator |\n| `--left` | The left position value |\n| `--top` | The top position value |\n| `--width` | The width of the element |\n| `--height` | The height of the element |\n\n\n**ItemControl Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the
